            World University Rankings        </h1>

						<div itemprop="articleBody">
							<article class="article">
								<p>RUR World University Rankings evaluate performance of 1000+ world’s leading higher
									education institutions by 20 indicators grouped into 4 key areas of university
									activity: Teaching, Research, International Diversity, Financial Sustainability. You
									can view the rankings for the period of 2010-2022 by selecting the year on the
									timeline and by choosing the ranking type in the menu below.</p>
								<p>Please also see <a href="/ranking/subject-rankings.html">RUR Subject Rankings</a>, <a href="/ranking/reputation-rankings.html">RUR Reputation Rankings</a>, <a href="/ranking/academic-rankings.html">RUR Academic Rankings</a>, <a href="/ranking/indicator_ranking.html">RUR Rankings by Indicators</a>.</p>
								<p>Please <a href="/methodology.html">click here</a> for methodological details.</p>
							</article>
